Output only the translation. <NL> English: like they've. <NL> French:	 comme ils l'ont <NL>  <NL> Explanation: In the French translations provided, you will notice that the reflexive pronouns (me, te, se, nous, vous, them) are often attached to the verb in the form of a single word.
